There is only one solution to a sudoku grid.\r\n\r\nSelect Create Grid if you want to work on a puzzle you have seen outside this game. Enter the layout of the puzzle on the blank grid and play the game normally.\r\n\r\nSelect Cheater if you just want to know the answer! Enter the layout of the puzzle you are stuck on into the blank grid. When you have entered the layout press the soft key indicator marked 'Solve' to see the correct answer.\r\n\r\nYou can write a list of possible numbers (candidates) for each empty cell to help you solve the grid. You can annotate empty cells with the pencil tool, which you can activate by pressing Pen/Pencil button. While in pencil mode, you can enter up to 6 candidates per cell.\r\n\r\nThe next easiest cell is highlighted in blue to help you solve the grid, however, if you do not want this on it can be turned off in options.\r\n\r\nIn the beginning of each game you receive some coins to pay for hints.
